           <h1 name="aa07" id="aa07" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--figure graf--title">5 Best JavaScript Frameworks in&nbsp;2017</h1>
           <p name="3768" id="3768" class="graf graf--p graf--hasDropCapModel graf--hasDropCap graf-after--h3"><span class="graf-dropCap">J</span>avaScript popularity continues its rising. In 2016 we’ve witnessed such great changes, as AngularJS entire upgrade and introduction of Angular 2, ultimate dominating of jQuery that is applied on <a href="https://w3techs.com/technologies/details/js-jquery/all/all" data-href="https://w3techs.com/technologies/details/js-jquery/all/all" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">96.5%</a> of all JS sites, evolution of ECMAScript, two updates of Node.js in April and October accordingly, React finest hours, and even more. What to expect from 2017??—?Here’s what we know so far: <a href="https://da-14.com/blog/how-will-angular-4-change-app-development" data-href="https://da-14.com/blog/how-will-angular-4-change-app-development" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Angular 4</a> is expected in March 2017, <a href="https://github.com/tc39/proposals/blob/master/finished-proposals.md" data-href="https://github.com/tc39/proposals/blob/master/finished-proposals.md" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">ES2017</a> edition is planned for mid-2017, Bootstrap v4 release should be anticipated this year as well.</p>
           <p name="a0c6" id="a0c6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Lately JavaScript was named among the best programming languages to learn in 2017 by <a href="https://www.ibm.com/developerworks/community/blogs/d13a8e32-0870-49cb-9b0d-ba0e34fa6561/entry/Which_Are_The_Best_Programming_Languages_to_Learn_in_2017?lang=en" data-href="https://www.ibm.com/developerworks/community/blogs/d13a8e32-0870-49cb-9b0d-ba0e34fa6561/entry/Which_Are_The_Best_Programming_Languages_to_Learn_in_2017?lang=en" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">IBM</a>. At this stage it is used on both client- and server-sides and helps to design flavorful interfaces, enrich web apps with numerous functions and features, modify web pages in real time and much more.</p>
           <p name="017b" id="017b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">In the meanwhile, JavaScript web frameworks can become a silver bullet for quick <a href="https://da-14.com/services/web-app-development" data-href="https://da-14.com/services/web-app-development" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">web app development</a>. They serve as a skeleton for single page apps, allow developers to worry less about code structure or maintenance while focusing on creation of complex interface elements, and expand opportunities of JS and plain HTML.</p>
           <h4 name="4f20" id="4f20" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">The advantages of using JavaScript frameworks:</h4>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="336f" id="336f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--h4"><strong class="markup--strong markup--li-strong">Efficiency?</strong>—?projects that used to take months and hundreds of lines of code now can be achieved much faster with well-structured prebuilt patterns and functions.</li>
            <li name="1321" id="1321" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><strong class="markup--strong markup--li-strong">Safety?</strong>—?top javascript frameworks have firm security arrangements and are supported by large communities where members and users also act as testers.</li>
            <li name="d51c" id="d51c" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><strong class="markup--strong markup--li-strong">Cost?</strong>—?most frameworks are open source and free. Since they help programmers to build custom solutions faster, the ultimate price for web app will be lower.</li>
           </ul>
           <h4 name="51be" id="51be" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--li">Best JavaScript frameworks in&nbsp;2017:</h4>
           <p name="b29c" id="b29c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Angular-s</strong></p>
           <figure name="0a58" id="0a58" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 394px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.3%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*tEHpEuutNvyFAT6-.jpg" data-width="1200" data-height="675" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*tEHpEuutNvyFAT6-.jpg">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*tEHpEuutNvyFAT6-.jpg?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*tEHpEuutNvyFAT6-.jpg">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*tEHpEuutNvyFAT6-.jpg">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="b647" id="b647" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">After a long-awaited release of Angular back in 2016, its popularity has touched new heights, though AngularJS will hold off on giving ground in 2017.</p>
           <p name="c4ec" id="c4ec" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Angular.js</strong> is often referred to as an MVW (Model-View-Whatever) framework and among the top benefits, for startups and mid-sized companies, people name: quick code production, easy testing of any app part and two-way data binding (changes in the backend are immediately reflected on the UI). Since release its ecosystem has gone beyond imagination. As for now, it is reasonably called the most used JS framework for SPAs (Single-Page Applications) development and it boasts the largest community of developers.</p>
           <p name="3d55" id="3d55" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Angular2 </strong>comes with a long list of features that enable building everything, ranging from web to desktop and mobile. Framework is built with TypeScript from Microsoft with an eye to making JavaScript more agile and attractive for large enterprises. ng2 features a component-based architecture, improved DI (dependency injection), efficient logging service, inter-component communications and more.</p>
           <p name="47e0" id="47e0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Both Angular-s are a better option for enterprise-based applications or for strict programming environments with high standards for code readability.</p>
           <p name="e336" id="e336" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">ReactJS</strong></p>
           <figure name="f990" id="f990" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 368px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 52.5%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*b9DhQIfCGxIBX0cp.jpg" data-width="1200" data-height="630" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*b9DhQIfCGxIBX0cp.jpg">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*b9DhQIfCGxIBX0cp.jpg?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*b9DhQIfCGxIBX0cp.jpg">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*b9DhQIfCGxIBX0cp.jpg">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="22a7" id="22a7" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">We’ve already made <a href="https://da-14.com/blog/reactjs-vs-angular-comparison-which-better" data-href="https://da-14.com/blog/reactjs-vs-angular-comparison-which-better" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">React and Angular comparison</a>, despite the fact that it is more of a library than a JS framework. It stands behind user interfaces of Facebook and Instagram, showing its efficiency within dynamic high-traffic applications.</p>
           <p name="a39b" id="a39b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">It is rightly considered the fastest growing JS framework: as of today, there are about 1,000 contributors on <a href="https://github.com/facebook/react" data-href="https://github.com/facebook/react" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Github</a>. In MVC (Model-View-Controller) pattern <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">React.js</strong> acts as “V” and can be smoothly integrated with any architecture. Due to the usage of virtual DOM it provides a great performance boost, comparing to Angular 1.x. In addition to that, React components can be created and re-used among applications or even transferred for public use.</p>
           <p name="d6dc" id="d6dc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Despite the fact that React has a higher learning curve, it makes app development straightforward and easy-to-understand. Furthermore it can be a perfect fit for complex, high-load and awesome software solutions.</p>
           <p name="2667" id="2667" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Vue.js</strong></p>
           <figure name="5bbf" id="5bbf" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 343px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 49%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*GTirD-bZIgi6Bef8.jpg" data-width="1200" data-height="588" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*GTirD-bZIgi6Bef8.jpg">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*GTirD-bZIgi6Bef8.jpg?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*GTirD-bZIgi6Bef8.jpg">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*GTirD-bZIgi6Bef8.jpg">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="05d6" id="05d6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Vue 2.0</strong> was also introduced in 2016 and it took the best from Ember, React and Angular, putting all that into a handy package. It is proved to be faster and leaner, comparing to React and Angular 2.0.</p>
           <p name="8090" id="8090" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Going deeper, Vue.js offers two-way data binding (seen in AngularJS), server-side rendering (like in Angular2 and ReactJS), Vue-cli (scaffolding tool for quick start) and optional JSX support. Its founder states that Vue 2 is one of the fastest frameworks all in all.</p>
           <p name="37f8" id="37f8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Vue.js is a better choice for quick development of cross-platform solutions. It can become a firm basis for high-end single page applications (SPAs) and beneficial solution to those cases, when performance is put ahead of good code organization or app structure.</p>
           <p name="1922" id="1922" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Ember.js</strong></p>
           <figure name="5a44" id="5a44" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 309px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 44.1%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*ZqR6mdu6O0Zr5hFg.png" data-width="1200" data-height="529" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*ZqR6mdu6O0Zr5hFg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*ZqR6mdu6O0Zr5hFg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*ZqR6mdu6O0Zr5hFg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*ZqR6mdu6O0Zr5hFg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="d4a8" id="d4a8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Back in 2015 Ember was called the best javascript framework for web application, leaving behind React and AngularJS. Today it boasts a huge online community, regular updates and wide appliance of JavaScript best practices to guarantee ultimate experience right out of the box.</p>
           <p name="df81" id="df81" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Ember </strong>features two-way data binding, like Angular.js, keeping both view and model in sync for all the time. Applying Fastboot.js module it ensures prompt server-side rendering of DOM, improving performance of complex UIs.</p>
           <p name="8620" id="8620" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Emberjs is commonly usable for complex feature-rich web applications and website. Among the top users are Chipotle, Blue Apron, Nordstrom, Kickstarter, LinkedIn, Netflix and many others. Moreover it has an easier learning curve and there are oceans of tutorials and guide available online.</p>
           <p name="598e" id="598e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Meteor.js</strong></p>
           <figure name="dd0d" id="dd0d" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 328px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 46.9%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*AYpgvU5hPD73DYWL.png" data-width="1024" data-height="480" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*AYpgvU5hPD73DYWL.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*AYpgvU5hPD73DYWL.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*AYpgvU5hPD73DYWL.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*AYpgvU5hPD73DYWL.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="3876" id="3876" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Meteor is among the most popular JavaScript frameworks but which comes well-heeled with tons of features for back-end development, front-end rendering, database management and business logic. Since release in 2012 its ecosystem has grown drastically and at a swift rate.</p>
           <p name="88b2" id="88b2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">This full-stack platform enables fast development of end-to-end web and mobile applications in pure JavaScript. Due to modular structure all the packages and libraries can be used at pace. In terms of performance, all the changes in the database are immediately transmitted to the UI and in conversely with no evident time losses caused by different languages or server response time.</p>
           <p name="b4a3" id="b4a3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">MeteorJS </strong>covers all the phases of software development cycle and takes care of such glooming processes as linking, files concatenation and others. It is of current usage in real-time application development for business companies like Mazda, IKEA, Honeywell and many others.</p>
           <h4 name="7f59" id="7f59" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">JavaScript framework comparison:</h4>

           <h4 name="97ef" id="97ef" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--figure">Conclusion</h4>
           <p name="0c3d" id="0c3d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">Taking an option on the right JavaScript framework is not about features that each can offer. It depends on initial company goals, project requirements, general framework functionality and how it can be applied within each particular case.</p>
           <p name="1a4d" id="1a4d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">When it comes to quick <a href="https://da-14.com/services/web-app-development" data-href="https://da-14.com/services/web-app-development" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">web development</a> or prototyping, JavaScript frameworks are among the most favorable and 2017 won’t become an exception. These frameworks and libraries have already reshaped the way how JS collaborates with HTML and CSS to compile views both in browsers and, by now, on native platforms.</p>
           <p name="61bf" id="61bf" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">This post originally appeared on DA-14 website.
